         <section class="zsg-content-section " id="hdp-neighborhood">
          <h2>
           Neighborhood: 29440
          </h2>
          <div class="zsg-content-component">
           <div class="za-track-event zsg-content-component notranslate" data-za-action="Market Guide - expand" data-za-category="Homes">
            Zillow predicts South Carolina home values will increase 1.5% next year. Among 29440 homes, this home is 5.8% less expensive than the midpoint (median) home, but is priced 6.1% more per square foot.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Foreclosures will be a
            <span class="hide" id="util_TextFold_0_toggleArea">
             factor impacting home values in the next several years.  In 29440, the number of foreclosures waiting to be sold is 4.2% higher than in Georgetown, and 29.5% less than the national average. This higher local number may prevent 29440 home values from rising as quickly as other regions in Georgetown.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             Learn more about
             <a href="https://zillow.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/203517190-How-are-Zillow-Home-Value-Forecasts-calculated-">
              forecast calculations
             </a>
             .
            </span>
